            <script>
                // Обработчик клика
                function productClick($itImpressions,trackId,floctory) {
                    // GTM
                    dataLayer.push({
                        "event": "productClick",
                        "ecommerce": {
                            "click": {
                                "actionField": {"list": "Карточка товара"},
                                "products": [$itImpressions]
                            }
                        }
                    });
                    // -------------------
                    // RR
                    (window["rrApiOnReady"] = window["rrApiOnReady"] || []).push(function() {
                        try{ rrApi.view($itImpressions.id_element); } catch(e) {}
                    });
                    // ----------------------

                    // TrackId
                    console.log(trackId);
                    tgCallEvent('product_view', trackId);
                }

                // Обработчик добавления в корзину
                function add2basket_catalog($itImpressions,trackId,floctory) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        'event': 'addToCart',
                        'ecommerce': {
                            'currencyCode': 'RUR',
                            'add': {
                                'actionField': {'list': 'Добавление товара в корзину'},
                                'products': [$itImpressions]
                            }
                        }
                    });
                    rrApi.addToBasket($itImpressions.id_element);
					//console.log('element start');
					//console.log ($itImpressions);
					//console.log('element end');
					//rrApi.addToBasket($itImpressions.id);

                    // TrackId
                    trackId.quantity = $("#inp_counter_srch_"+trackId.id).val();
                    tgCallEvent('product_add', trackId);
                }

                // Перейти в корзину.
                function getToBasketHandler(itImpressions) {
                    dataLayer.push({
                        "event": "getBasketClick",
                        "ecommerce": {
                            "click": {
                                "actionField": {"list": "Переход в корзину"},
                                "products": [itImpressions]
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }

                // При загрузке страницы.
                /*var allStartPageImpressions = ;
                 if (allStartPageImpressions.length > 0) {
                 dataLayer.push({
                 'ecommerce': {
                 'currencyCode': 'RUR',
                 'impressions': allStartPageImpressions
                 }
                 });
                 }*/
            </script>

                </script>

<script>
	//всплывашка 
	
	templata_hover_link = '<div class="a_hover_link"><a href="#">Перейти в раздел</a></div>';
	
	function remove_hover_link (){
		$('.a_hover_link').remove();
	}
	
	timerId = '';
	
	$( document ).ready(function() {
		$( "#left_search_block_filter .nav-filter li" ).hover(function() {
			if ($(this).attr('data-get_params')){
				position = $(this).position();
				width = $('#left_search_block_filter').outerWidth() - 2;
				if ($('.a_hover_link').length > 0){
					height_of_el = $('.a_hover_link').outerHeight();
					height_of_block = $(this).height();
					$('.a_hover_link').css('top', position.top - (height_of_el/2 - height_of_block/2));
					$('.a_hover_link').css('left', position.left + width);
					$('.a_hover_link a').attr('href', $(this).attr('url-data'));
					
					oldTimerId = timerId;
					clearTimeout(oldTimerId);
					timerId = setTimeout(remove_hover_link, 4000);
					
				} else {
					$('#left_search_block_filter').append(templata_hover_link);
					height_of_el = $('.a_hover_link').outerHeight();
					height_of_block = $(this).height();
					$('.a_hover_link').css('top', position.top - (height_of_el/2 - height_of_block/2));
					$('.a_hover_link').css('left', position.left + width);
					$('.a_hover_link a').attr('href', $(this).attr('url-data'));
					
					oldTimerId = timerId;
					clearTimeout(oldTimerId);
					timerId = setTimeout(remove_hover_link, 4000);
				}
			} 
		});
	});
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).ready(function () {
            $(".ymap-search, #street_text, #house_text, #datepicker, label[for=cartFloor], label[for=move_distance], .lift_mark .minus, .lift_mark .plus, .lift_mark .counter, .select-gray, input[name=carry_value], label[for=paymentSite7cartShip], label[for=paymentSite8cartShip], label[for=paymentSite9cartShip]").click(function () {
                empty_delivery_block();
            });

            $(".ymap-search").change(function () {
                if (($('.ymap-search').val() != '') && ($('#street_text').val() != '')) {
                    $('#map_zone').val('');
                    $('#over_zone_value').val('');
                    $('#PosYandex').val('');
                }

                $('#house_text').val('');
                $('.ymap-search-submit').show();
                $('#house_text').show();

            });

            $("#price-delivery-form-id #datepicker").keydown(function (e) {
                keys = {
                    LCLICK: 91,
                    RCLICK: 92
                };
                if ((e.which != keys.LCLICK) && (e.which != keys.RCLICK)) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                }
            });
        });

        function empty_delivery_block() {
            $('#transport-deli-json').html('0,00');
            $('#transfer-deli-json').html('0,00');
            $('#lifting-deli-json').html('0,00');
            $('#total-deli-json').html('0,00');
            $('#deli-sum-row').html('0,00');
            $('#total-sum-row').html('0,00');
            $('#price_delivery_serv_hid').val('0,00');
            $('#price_lifting_serv_hid').val('0,00');
            $('#price_transfer_serv_hid').val('0,00');
            $('#price_delivery_all_serv_hid').val('0,00');
        }

        function AjaxFormRequest(result_id, form_id, url,region='') {

            var can_i = true;
            var datepckr = true;
            if ($('#city_text').val() == '') {
                can_i = false;
            }
            if ($('#street_text').val() == '') {
                can_i = false;
            }
            if ($('#house_text').val() == '') {
                can_i = false;
            }
            
            /*if ($('#datepicker').val() == '') {
                can_i = false;
            }*/

            if(region.length != '' && region == 'moscow'){

            }else{
                if ($('#datepicker').val() == '') {
                    datepckr = false;
                }
            }

            if (can_i == true) {
                jQuery.ajax({
                    url: url,
                    type: "POST",
                    dataType: "JSON",
                    data: jQuery("#" + form_id).serialize(),
                    success: function (response) {

                        if(region.length != '' && region == 'moscow'){

                            if($("#res_sdek_mess").text() != ''){
                                $("#res_sdek_mess").text('');
                                $("#res_sdek_mess").hide();
                            }

                            if(response.status == 'Y'){
                                $('#total-deli-json').html(response.result.price);
                                $('#price_delivery_all_serv_hid').val(response.result.price);
                            }else{
                                $('#total-deli-json').html('0');
                                $('#price_delivery_all_serv_hid').val('0');
                                if(response.mess != ''){
                                    $("#res_sdek_mess").html(response.mess);
                                    $("#res_sdek_mess").show();
                                }
                            }

                        }else{
                            if (response.ErrorDelivery[0] == 'false ') {
                                $('#transport-deli-json').html(response.PriceDeliveryTransport[0]);
                                $('#transfer-deli-json').html(response.PriceDeliveryTransfer[0]);
                                $('#lifting-deli-json').html(response.PriceDeliveryLift[0]);
                                $('#total-deli-json').html(response.PriceDeliveryTotal[0]);
                                $('#deli-sum-row').html(response.lineStrSum);

                                //new: добавим в св-ва заказа стоимость транспортировки, переноса, подъёма:
                                $('#price_delivery_serv_hid').val(response.PriceDeliveryTransport[0]);
                                $('#price_lifting_serv_hid').val(response.PriceDeliveryLift[0]);
                                $('#price_transfer_serv_hid').val(response.PriceDeliveryTransfer[0]);
                                $('#price_delivery_all_serv_hid').val(response.PriceDeliveryTotal[0]);
                                //--new

                                var sum_info = $('#total-sum-items').text();
                                sum_info = sum_info.replace(' ', '');
                                var sum_info_num_item = parseInt(sum_info);
                                var sum_info_num_deli = parseInt(response.lineStrSum);

                                //var total_vr = sum_info_num_item + sum_info_num_deli;
                                //total_vr = formatPrice(total_vr);


                                //$('#total-sum-row').html(total_vr+'<q>,-</q>');

                            } else {
                                $('#transport-deli-json').html('0 ');
                                $('#transfer-deli-json').html('0 ');
                                $('#lifting-deli-json').html('0 ');
                                $('#total-deli-json').html('0 ');
                                $('#deli-sum-row').html('0 ');
                                $('#total-sum-row').html('0 ');

                            }
                        }
                    }

                })
            } else if (can_i == false && datepckr == true) {
                //
                $('html, body').animate({scrollTop: $(".ya-maps-block").offset().top}, "slow");
                
                $('#warning_zone').show('slow');
                setTimeout(function() {$('#warning_zone').hide('slow');}, 10000);
                return false;
                //
            } else if (can_i == true && datepckr == false){
                $("input[name='date']").addClass('error');
                setTimeout(function() { $("input[name='date']").removeClass('error') }, 1000);
                return false;
            } else {
                $('html, body').animate({scrollTop: $(".ya-maps-block").offset().top}, "slow");
                $('#warning_zone').show('slow');
                setTimeout(function() {$('#warning_zone').hide('slow');}, 10000);
                $("input[name='date']").addClass('error');
                setTimeout(function() { $("input[name='date']").removeClass('error') }, 1000);
                return false;
            }
        }
    </script>
